A delusion that oneself or the world, or parts thereof, have ceased to exist. <br>5. (Russia) Alternative letter-case form of Nihilism <br>6. A doctrine grounded on the negation of one or more meaningful aspects of life; in particular, the view that nothing in the world actually exists. <br>7. Something that is regarded as meaningless. <br>	1
